CREATE TABLE lessons(id UUID PRIMARY KEY, lesson_name STRING, course_id UUID REFERENCES courses(id), lesson_content TEXT);

CREATE TABLE courses(id UUID PRIMARY KEY, course_name STRING, instructor STRING, start_date DATE, end_date DATE);</t><s>SELECT * FROM courses JOIN lessons ON courses.id = lessons.course_id WHERE courses.course_name = 'Math';</s>

CREATE TABLE lessons(id UUID PRIMARY KEY, lesson_name STRING, course_id UUID REFERENCES courses(id), lesson_content TEXT);</t><s>SELECT course_name, lesson_name FROM courses JOIN lessons ON courses.id = lessons.course_id;</s>
